# Prime Consensus Patterns

The combinators of consensus. Every ratio a/b for body sizes 1 through 100
where a ≥ 1. Each ratio is a governance position — from a single fragment
through unanimous consent.

1/3 is not a minimum threshold. 1/3 is the diffusion of one admin into three
dictators — each holds 1/3, none holds majority. It creates three dictators,
not one. The consensus begins when 2/3 agree.

See [CONSENSUS_MATHEMATICS.md](CONSENSUS_MATHEMATICS.md) for full theory.

| # | a/1 | % | Class |
|---|-------|---|-------|
| 1 | 1/1 | 100.0% | unanimous |
